msg:We stopped for a short break and checked in after dark. The surrounding area is not too lively, and there is no public transportation, which is inconvenient to travel.
The hotel seems to have been owned by Kaiyuan Group before. The parking lot is quite large, and there is a fountain at the door. The room hardware is really good. The upgraded parent-child family room is huge and has a bathtub and smart toilet. The shower room, toilet, and sink are all independent. The bedding is also very comfortable.
The details or software of the hotel are really not as good as the hardware!
Service: There are several incredible operations. 1. Before checking in, there was a call asking when to arrive (the call was received at 18:00, and the room could be cancelled before 20:00); 2. Before 12:00, they called to ask if you would like to extend your stay. If you donâ€™t want to extend your stay, they asked you when to check out (the room is checked out before 14:00). 3. I originally booked a twin room, which was upgraded for free when I checked in. I was very happy. After completing the formalities, they told me that the room was on the top floor and the elevator was not enough and I needed to climb one flight of stairs (why didnâ€™t they tell me before the formalities?) I was instantly unhappy.
Facilities: The room has everything it should have, but it is extremely unscientific and uncoordinated. The room phone is next to the child's bed; the swing blocks the sofa and water bar; there is no master switch next to the bed; there is only one trash can in the huge room: the furniture in the family room is business-style. The wifi name is not the hotel's.
Breakfast: That was quite unsatisfactory! The meal was finished at 9 o'clock, and many were gone after 8 o'clock. The variety of dishes is OK, but the quality is not high. The coffee is instant two-in-one directly from the machine, the juice is completely technological, the grilled sausage is definitely starchy, and the cabbage is fried. It is worth mentioning that there are braised pork and millet soup! The freshly cooked noodles are also delicious. The first time I saw a buffet restaurant with all big round tables, I wanted to say: If you are hosting a wedding banquet, you can completely not open breakfast!
Overall, the experience is not good!
